+        item = "supplementary figure 87" + suffix
+        if item in SELSET:
+            add_supp(item, ["G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"], "iv", method, "supp87", target="serum")
+            copy = dict(ROWS[-1])
+            copy["Route_of_administration"] = "intratumoral"
+            ROWS.append(copy)
+    if "supplementary figure 88" in SELSET:
+        add_supp("supplementary figure 88", tox_groups, "iv", "ELISA_AST_ALT", "supp88", target="serum")
+    if "supplementary figure 89" in SELSET:
+        add_supp("supplementary figure 89", tox_groups, "invivo", "ELISA_AST_ALT", "supp89", target="serum")
+
+    if "figure 5h" in SELSET:
+        row = base_row("figure 5h", "scatterplot", "low")
+        cond_invivo(row, "tumor", "RNA-seq")
+        apply_formulation(row, "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP")
+        row["evidence_text"] = EVID["fig5h"] + " " + EVID["fig5"]
+        row["evidence_image"] = row["source_image"]
+        row["manual_required"] = "true"
+        row["reason"] = "Selected volcano plot does not provide a row-level formulation/value context in Stage 06; retained as manual-review placeholder."
+        add(row)
+
+    represented = {r["Item_ID"].lower() for r in ROWS}
+    for _, selected in SELECTED.iterrows():
+        if selected.item_id.lower() not in represented:
+            row = base_row(clean(selected.item_id), clean(selected.visual_type), "low")
+            add_excel(row, clean(selected.item_id))
+            row["evidence_text"] = clean(selected.reason)
+            row["evidence_image"] = row["source_image"]
+            row["manual_required"] = "true"
+            row["reason"] = "Selected item lacked deterministic condition/formulation extraction rules; placeholder row retained for manual review."
+            add(row)
+
+
+def finalize():
+    for row in ROWS:
+        for col in SMILES_COLS:
+            row[col] = ""
+        if row["Model"] and row["Model"] not in {"in_vitro", "in_vivo", "ex_vivo", "N/A"}:
+            row["Model"] = ""
+            row["manual_required"] = "true"
+            row["reason"] = (row["reason"] + " Invalid Model normalized blank.").strip()
+        if row["metric_type"] and not (row["evidence_excel"] or row["excel_file"] or row["block_csv_path"]):
+            for col in ["metric_type", "original_values", "aggregated_value", "unit", "replicate_type"]:
+                row[col] = ""
+            row["reason"] = (row["reason"] + " Numeric value fields blanked because no Excel/source-data provenance was mapped.").strip()
+
+    stamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
+    for name in ["unified_extraction.csv", "unified_extraction.json", "unified_extraction_review_flags.csv"]:
+        path = os.path.join(BASE, name)
+        if os.path.exists(path):
+            shutil.copy2(path, path + ".bak_" + stamp)
+
+    pd.DataFrame(ROWS, columns=COLUMNS).to_csv(os.path.join(BASE, "unified_extraction.csv"), index=False, encoding="utf-8-sig")
+
+    flags = []
+    for row in ROWS:
+        if row["manual_required"] == "true":
+            flags.append([PAPER_ID, row["Item_ID"], row["block_id"], "row", "manual_required", "medium", row["reason"] or "Manual review requested."])
+        if not row["evidence_image"]:
+            flags.append([PAPER_ID, row["Item_ID"], row["block_id"], "evidence_image", "missing_figure_evidence", "low", "No source image was available in total_figure_mapping.json."])
+        if not row["Formulation_Name"]:
+            flags.append([PAPER_ID, row["Item_ID"], row["block_id"], "Formulation_Name", "missing_formulation", "medium", "No concise formulation/control label could be extracted."])
+        if not row["Model"]:
+            flags.append([PAPER_ID, row["Item_ID"], row["block_id"], "Model", "missing_condition", "medium", "No concise model context could be extracted."])
+    flags = [list(x) for x in dict.fromkeys(tuple(f) for f in flags)]
+    pd.DataFrame(flags, columns=["Paper_ID", "Item_ID", "block_id", "field", "issue", "severity", "reason"]).to_csv(
+        os.path.join(BASE, "unified_extraction_review_flags.csv"), index=False, encoding="utf-8-sig"
+    )
+
+    summary = {
+        "paper_id": PAPER_ID,
+        "paper_folder": BASE,
+        "stage": "06_unified_lnpdb_extraction",
+        "created_at": datetime.now().isoformat(timespec="seconds"),
+        "record_count": len(ROWS),
+        "selected_item_count": int(len(SELECTED)),
+        "represented_item_count": len({r["Item_ID"].lower() for r in ROWS}),
+        "excel_value_rows": sum(1 for r in ROWS if r["metric_type"]),
+        "smiles_policy": "IL_SMILES, HL_SMILES, CHL_SMILES, PEG_SMILES, and Fifth_component_SMILES intentionally blank for Stage 06.",
+        "sources": [
+            "fig_table_lnpdb_classified.csv",
+            "total_figure_mapping.json",
+            "excel_mapping.json",
+            "excel_mapping_rows.csv",
+            "excel_block_inventory.csv",
+            "QS_2026/QS_2026.md",
+            "41565_2025_2102_MOESM1_ESM/41565_2025_2102_MOESM1_ESM.md",
+        ],
+    }
+    with open(os.path.join(BASE, "unified_extraction.json"), "w", encoding="utf-8") as handle:
+        json.dump({"source_summary": summary, "records": ROWS}, handle, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
+    print(json.dumps(summary, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
+    print("flags", len(flags))
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    generate()
+    finalize()

+    "fig5h": "Fig. 5h is a volcano plot from bulk RNA-seq comparing treatment with control; it was selected but lacks a formulation-level scalar metric suitable for current Stage 06 extraction.",
+}
+
+
+def clean(x):
+    if x is None or (isinstance(x, float) and math.isnan(x)):
+        return ""
+    s = str(x).strip()
+    if s.lower() in {"nan", "none"}:
+        return ""
+    return s.replace("GO-", "G0-").replace("G0-6C-AA_C12", "G0-6C-AA-C12")
+
+
+def load_context():
+    cls = pd.read_csv(os.path.join(BASE, "fig_table_lnpdb_classified.csv"))
+    selected = cls[cls["manual_select"].astype(str).str.lower().eq("yes")].copy()
+    xrows = pd.read_csv(os.path.join(BASE, "excel_mapping_rows.csv"))
+    by_item = {}
+    for _, row in xrows.iterrows():
+        by_item.setdefault(clean(row.get("pdf_item_id")).lower(), []).append(row.to_dict())
+    with open(os.path.join(BASE, "total_figure_mapping.json"), encoding="utf-8") as handle:
+        raw_map = json.load(handle)
+    figmap, source_doc = {}, {}
+    for doc, items in raw_map.items():
+        for item, meta in items.items():
+            figmap[item.lower()] = meta
+            source_doc[item.lower()] = doc
+    return selected, by_item, figmap, source_doc
+
+
+SELECTED, EXCEL_BY_ITEM, FIGMAP, SOURCE_DOC = load_context()
+SELSET = set(SELECTED.item_id.str.lower())
+
+
+def base_row(item, visual_type, confidence="high"):
+    meta = FIGMAP.get(item.lower(), {})
+    row = {c: "" for c in COLUMNS}
+    row.update({
+        "Paper_ID": PAPER_ID,
+        "Item_ID": item,
+        "visual_type": visual_type,
+        "source_type": SOURCE_DOC.get(item.lower(), ""),
+        "source_image": clean(meta.get("source_image")),
+        "source_pdf": clean(meta.get("source_pdf")),
+        "source_page": clean(meta.get("source_page")),
+        "selected_source_for_paneling": clean(meta.get("selected_source_for_paneling")),
+        "Experiment_batching": "individual",
+        "confidence": confidence,
+        "manual_required": "false",
+    })
+    return row
+
+
+def excel_for(item):
+    rows = EXCEL_BY_ITEM.get(item.lower(), [])
+    if not rows:
+        return {}
+    row = rows[0]
+    return {k: clean(row.get(k)) for k in ["excel_file", "excel_sheet", "block_id", "block_csv_path", "evidence_excel"]}
+
+
+def add_excel(row, item):
+    meta = excel_for(item)
+    for k in ["excel_file", "excel_sheet", "block_id", "block_csv_path"]:
+        row[k] = meta.get(k, "")
+    row["evidence_excel"] = meta.get("evidence_excel", "")
+
+
+def apply_formulation(row, label):
+    label = clean(label)
+    row["Formulation_Name"] = label
+    if not label:
+        return
+    if label.upper() == "PBS":
+        row["formulation_id"] = "QS_2026_CTRL_PBS"
+        return
+    if "free IL-12 mRNA" in label:
+        row["formulation_id"] = "QS_2026_CTRL_FREE_IL12_mRNA"
+        row["Cargo"], row["Cargo_type"] = "mRNA", "IL-12"
+        return
+    if "free IDO" in label:
+        row["formulation_id"] = "QS_2026_CTRL_FREE_IDO"
+        row["Fifth_component_name"] = "indoximod"
+        return
+    lipid = label
+    for suffix in [" FLuc pLNP", " FLuc LNP", " IL-12 pLNP", " IL-12 LNP", " pLNP", " LNP"]:
+        lipid = lipid.replace(suffix, "")
+    lipid = lipid.strip()
+    if label == "MC3" or lipid == "MC3":
+        row["formulation_id"] = "QS_2026_F_MC3"
+        row["IL_name"], row["HL_name"] = "DLin-MC3-DMA", "DSPC"
+    else:
+        row["formulation_id"] = "QS_2026_F_" + re.sub(r"[^A-Za-z0-9]+", "_", lipid).strip("_")
+        row["IL_name"], row["HL_name"] = lipid, "DOPE"
+    row["IL_molarratio"], row["HL_molarratio"] = "50", "10"
+    row["CHL_name"], row["CHL_molarratio"] = "Cholesterol", "38.5"
+    row["PEG_name"], row["PEG_molarratio"] = "DMG-PEG2000", "1.5"
+    if "IL-12" in label:
+        row["Cargo"], row["Cargo_type"] = "mRNA", "IL-12"
+    elif "FLuc" in label:
+        row["Cargo"], row["Cargo_type"] = "mRNA", "FLuc"
+
+
+def cond_screen(row, model="MC38", dose="0.05", method="luminescence"):
+    row.update({
+        "Aqueous_buffer": "10 mM citrate buffer pH 3",
+        "Dialysis_buffer": "PBS",
+        "Mixing_method": "pipette",
+        "Model": "in_vitro",
+        "Model_type": model,
+        "Model_target": "in_vitro",
+        "Route_of_administration": "in_vitro",
+        "Cargo": "mRNA",
+        "Cargo_type": "FLuc",
+        "Dose_ug_nucleicacid": dose,
+        "Experiment_method": method,
+    })
+
+
+def cond_micro(row, model, method, cargo_type="IL-12"):
+    row.update({
+        "Aqueous_buffer": "10 mM citrate buffer pH 3",
+        "Dialysis_buffer": "PBS",
+        "Mixing_method": "microfluidic",
+        "Model": "in_vitro",
+        "Model_type": model,
+        "Model_target": "in_vitro",
+        "Route_of_administration": "in_vitro",
+        "Cargo": "mRNA" if cargo_type else "",
+        "Cargo_type": cargo_type,
+        "Experiment_method": method,
+        "condition_1_name": "mRNA_concentration",
+        "condition_1_value": "0.5 ug/mL",
+    })
+
+
+def cond_invivo(row, target, method, route="intratumoral"):
+    row.update({
+        "Aqueous_buffer": "10 mM citrate buffer pH 3",
+        "Dialysis_buffer": "PBS",
+        "Mixing_method": "microfluidic",
+        "Model": "in_vivo",
+        "Model_type": "Mouse_MC38_tumor",
+        "Model_target": target,
+        "Route_of_administration": route,
+        "Cargo": "mRNA",
+        "Dose_ug_nucleicacid": "2.5",
+        "Experiment_method": method,
+    })
+
+
+def set_metric(row, metric, values, unit=""):
+    vals = []
+    for value in values:
+        try:
+            if not pd.isna(value):
+                vals.append(float(value))
+        except Exception:
+            pass
+    if not vals:
+        return
+    row["metric_type"] = metric
+    row["original_values"] = "|".join(f"{v:g}" for v in vals)
+    row["aggregated_value"] = f"{sum(vals) / len(vals):.10g}"
+    row["unit"] = unit
+    row["replicate_type"] = "biological_replicate"
+    row["reason"] = (row["reason"] + " Arithmetic mean computed from unambiguous replicate columns in mapped Excel block.").strip()
+
+
+def read_block(relpath):
+    return pd.read_csv(os.path.join(BASE, relpath), header=None)
+
+
+def group_values(relpath):
+    df = read_block(relpath)
+    if clean(df.iloc[0, 0]).startswith("Fig."):
+        labels = [clean(x) for x in df.iloc[1].tolist()]
+        values = df.iloc[2].tolist() if len(df) > 2 else []
+    else:
+        labels = [clean(x) for x in df.iloc[0].tolist()]
+        values = df.iloc[1].tolist() if len(df) > 1 else []
+    out = {}
+    for label, value in zip(labels, values):
+        if label and not label.startswith("Fig."):
+            out.setdefault(label, []).append(value)
+    return out
+
+
+ROWS = []
+
+
+def add(row):
+    for col in SMILES_COLS:
+        row[col] = ""
+    if str(row["manual_required"]).lower() in {"true", "1"}:
+        row["manual_required"] = "true"
+    else:
+        row["manual_required"] = "false"
+    ROWS.append({c: row.get(c, "") for c in COLUMNS})
+
+
+def visual_type(item):
+    hit = SELECTED[SELECTED.item_id.str.lower().eq(item.lower())]
+    return clean(hit.iloc[0]["visual_type"]) if not hit.empty else ""
+
+
+def add_configured_item(item, groups, cond, method, evidence, metric="", unit="", target="tumor", route="intratumoral"):
+    vals = {}
+    excel = excel_for(item)
+    if excel.get("block_csv_path"):
+        try:
+            vals = group_values(excel["block_csv_path"])
+        except Exception:
+            vals = {}
+    for group in groups:
+        row = base_row(item, visual_type(item))
+        add_excel(row, item)
+        if cond == "fig2c":
+            cond_invivo(row, "tumor", method)
+            row["Cargo_type"] = "FLuc"
+        elif cond == "fig3":
+            cond_micro(row, "MC38", method, "IL-12")
+        elif cond == "fig3t":
+            cargo = "IL-12" if "IL-12" in group else ("FLuc" if "FLuc" in group else "")
+            cond_micro(row, "MC38-OVA", method, cargo)
+            row["Dose_ug_nucleicacid"] = "0.5"
+            row["condition_1_name"], row["condition_1_value"] = "co_culture", "MC38-OVA_OT-I_CD3_T_cells"
+        elif cond == "invivo":
+            cond_invivo(row, target, method, route)
+        apply_formulation(row, group)
+        if "IL-12" in group:
+            row["Cargo"], row["Cargo_type"] = "mRNA", "IL-12"
+        elif "FLuc" in group or group == "MC3":
+            row["Cargo"], row["Cargo_type"] = "mRNA", "FLuc"
+        row["evidence_text"] = EVID[evidence] + " " + EVID["prep"]
+        row["evidence_image"] = row["source_image"]
+        for candidate in [group, group.replace(" pLNP", "").replace(" LNP", ""), group.replace(" Fluc", " FLuc"), group.replace("FLuc", "Fluc")]:
+            if candidate in vals:
+                set_metric(row, metric, vals[candidate], unit)
+                break
+        add(row)
+
+
+def add_supp(item, groups, condkind, method, evidence, target="in_vitro", route="intratumoral", model="MC38", confidence="medium"):
+    for group in groups:
+        row = base_row(item, visual_type(item), confidence)
+        if condkind == "screen_hepg2":
+            cond_screen(row, "HepG2", "0.05", method)
+        elif condkind == "screen_mc38":
+            cond_screen(row, "MC38", "", method)
+            row["condition_1_name"], row["condition_1_value"] = "mRNA_concentration", "500 ng/mL"
+        elif condkind == "micro":
+            cond_micro(row, model, method, "IL-12" if "IL-12" in group or method != "pKa" else "FLuc")
+        elif condkind == "tcell":
+            cargo = "IL-12" if "IL-12" in group else ("FLuc" if "FLuc" in group else "")
+            cond_micro(row, "primary_mouse_CD3_T_cells", method, cargo)
+            row["condition_1_name"], row["condition_1_value"] = "MC38_conditioned_supernatant", "1:1 with T cell medium"
+        elif condkind in {"invivo", "iv"}:
+            cond_invivo(row, target, method, "intravenous" if condkind == "iv" else route)
+        apply_formulation(row, group)
+        if "IL-12" in group:
+            row["Cargo"], row["Cargo_type"] = "mRNA", "IL-12"
+        elif "FLuc" in group or "MC3" in group:
+            row["Cargo"], row["Cargo_type"] = "mRNA", "FLuc"
+        row["evidence_text"] = EVID[evidence] + " " + EVID["prep"]
+        row["evidence_image"] = row["source_image"]
+        if evidence == "supp52":
+            row["manual_required"] = "true"
+            row["reason"] = "Figure/table image contains characterization values, but Stage 06 does not extract numeric values from images or captions without Excel provenance."
+        add(row)
+
+
+def generate():
+    lib_heads = ["P2A-SS-AA", "T3A-SS-AA", "G0-SS-AA", "110-SS-AA", "306-SS-AA", "L2A-SS-AA", "DAB-SS-AA"]
+    if "figure 2b" in SELSET:
+        item = "figure 2b"
+        rel = excel_for(item).get("block_csv_path", "")
+        df = read_block(rel)
+        for i in range(1, len(df)):
+            head = clean(df.iloc[i, 0])
+            for tail, start in [("C10", 1), ("C12", 4), ("C14", 7)]:
+                name = f"{head}-{tail}"
+                row = base_row(item, "heatmap")
+                add_excel(row, item)
+                cond_screen(row, "MC38", "0.05", "luminescence")
+                apply_formulation(row, name)
+                row["evidence_text"] = EVID["fig2"] + " " + EVID["prep"]
+                row["evidence_image"] = row["source_image"]
+                set_metric(row, "luminescence", df.iloc[i, start:start + 3].tolist(), "RLU")
+                add(row)
+
+    configs = {
+        "figure 2c": (["G0-SS-AA-C10", "G0-SS-AA-C12", "G0-SS-AA-C14", "G0-6C-AA-C12", "MC3"], "fig2c", "IVIS", "fig2", "luminescence", "total flux", "tumor"),
+        "figure 3b": (["MC3", "G0-6C-AA-C12", "G0-SS-AA-C12"], "fig3", "ELISA_IL-12_secreted", "fig3_elisa", "secreted_IL-12", "ng/mL", "in_vitro"),
+        "figure 3c": (["MC3", "G0-6C-AA-C12", "G0-SS-AA-C12"], "fig3", "ELISA_IL-12_intracellular", "fig3_elisa", "intracellular_IL-12", "ng/mL", "in_vitro"),
+        "figure 3e": (["MC3", "G0-6C-AA-C12", "G0-SS-AA-C12"], "fig3", "fluorescence_IL-12_MFI", "fig3_elisa", "fluorescence_MFI", "MFI", "in_vitro"),
+        "figure 3i": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 FLuc pLNP", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"], "fig3t", "flow_cytometry_CD69_T_cells", "fig3_tcell", "CD69_positive_T_cells", "%", "in_vitro"),
+        "figure 3j": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 FLuc pLNP", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"], "fig3t", "flow_cytometry_CD25_T_cells", "fig3_tcell", "CD25_positive_T_cells", "%", "in_vitro"),
+        "figure 3k": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 FLuc pLNP", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"], "fig3t", "flow_cytometry_PD-1_T_cells", "fig3_tcell", "PD-1_positive_T_cells", "%", "in_vitro"),
+        "figure 4g": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 Fluc", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12"], "invivo", "flow_cytometry_CD8_T_cells", "fig4", "CD8_T_cells", "%", "spleen"),
+        "figure 4h": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 Fluc", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12"], "invivo", "flow_cytometry_CD4_T_cells", "fig4", "CD4_T_cells", "%", "spleen"),
+        "figure 4i": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 Fluc", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12"], "invivo", "flow_cytometry_CD8_effector_memory_T_cells", "fig4", "CD8_effector_memory_T_cells", "%", "spleen"),
+        "figure 4j": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 Fluc", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12"], "invivo", "flow_cytometry_CD4_effector_memory_T_cells", "fig4", "CD4_effector_memory_T_cells", "%", "spleen"),
+        "figure 4k": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 Fluc", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12"], "invivo", "flow_cytometry_CD8_central_memory_T_cells", "fig4", "CD8_central_memory_T_cells", "%", "spleen"),
+        "figure 4l": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 Fluc", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12"], "invivo", "flow_cytometry_CD4_central_memory_T_cells", "fig4", "CD4_central_memory_T_cells", "%", "spleen"),
+        "figure 4m": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 Fluc", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12"], "invivo", "flow_cytometry_regulatory_T_cells", "fig4", "regulatory_T_cells", "%", "spleen"),
+        "figure 5b": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 Fluc", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12"], "invivo", "flow_cytometry_tumor_CD8_T_cells", "fig5", "tumor_CD8_T_cells", "%", "tumor"),
+        "figure 5c": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 Fluc", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12"], "invivo", "flow_cytometry_tumor_CD4_T_cells", "fig5", "tumor_CD4_T_cells", "%", "tumor"),
+        "figure 5d": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 Fluc", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12"], "invivo", "flow_cytometry_PD-1_CD8_T_cells", "fig5", "PD-1_CD8_T_cells", "%", "tumor"),
+        "figure 5e": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 Fluc", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12"], "invivo", "flow_cytometry_PD-1_CD4_T_cells", "fig5", "PD-1_CD4_T_cells", "%", "tumor"),
+        "figure 5f": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 FLuc pLNP", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12 LNP", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"], "invivo", "ELISA_TNF-alpha", "fig5", "TNF-alpha", "pg/mL", "tumor"),
+        "figure 5g": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 FLuc pLNP", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12 LNP", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"], "invivo", "ELISA_IFN-gamma", "fig5", "IFN-gamma", "pg/mL", "tumor"),
+        "figure 5i": (["G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12"], "invivo", "qPCR_IFN-gamma", "fig5", "IFN-gamma_fold_change", "fold_change", "tumor"),
+        "figure 6k": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 Fluc pLNP", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12 LNP", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"], "invivo", "flow_cytometry_contralateral_tumor_CD8_T_cells", "fig6", "contralateral_tumor_CD8_T_cells", "%", "tumor"),
+        "figure 6l": (["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 Fluc pLNP", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12 LNP", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"], "invivo", "flow_cytometry_contralateral_tumor_CD4_T_cells", "fig6", "contralateral_tumor_CD4_T_cells", "%", "tumor"),
+    }
+    for item, cfg in configs.items():
+        if item in SELSET:
+            add_configured_item(item, *cfg)
+
+    for item, method in [("figure 6b", "tumor_volume"), ("figure 6c", "tumor_volume_individual"), ("figure 6d", "survival")]:
+        if item in SELSET:
+            for group in ["Control group", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"]:
+                row = base_row(item, visual_type(item), "medium" if item == "figure 6d" else "high")
+                add_excel(row, item)
+                cond_invivo(row, "tumor", method)
+                apply_formulation(row, group)
+                if group == "Control group":
+                    row["formulation_id"], row["Cargo"], row["Cargo_type"] = "QS_2026_CTRL_RECHALLENGE", "", ""
+                row["evidence_text"] = EVID["fig6"] + " " + EVID["prep"]
+                row["evidence_image"] = row["source_image"]
+                if item == "figure 6d":
+                    row["manual_required"], row["reason"] = "true", "No exact Excel source-data block was mapped for the selected survival panel."
+                add(row)
+
+    lib21 = [f"{h}-{t}" for h in lib_heads for t in ["C10", "C12", "C14"]]
+    if "supplementary figure 47" in SELSET:
+        add_supp("supplementary figure 47", lib21, "screen_hepg2", "luminescence", "supp47", model="HepG2")
+    if "supplementary figure 49" in SELSET:
+        add_supp("supplementary figure 49", lib21, "screen_mc38", "cell_viability_normalized", "supp49")
+    for item, group, method in [
+        ("supplementary figure 52c", "G0-SS-AA-C12 pLNP", "physicochemical_characterization"),
+        ("supplementary figure 53c", "G0-6C-AA-C12 LNP", "physicochemical_characterization"),
+        ("supplementary figure 54a", "G0-SS-AA-C12 pLNP", "pKa"),
+        ("supplementary figure 54b", "G0-6C-AA-C12 LNP", "pKa"),
+        ("supplementary figure 59", "G0-SS-AA-C12 pLNP", "HPLC_indoximod_release"),
+    ]:
+        if item in SELSET:
+            add_supp(item, [group], "micro", method, "supp52")
+    if "supplementary figure 56b" in SELSET:
+        add_supp("supplementary figure 56b", ["MC3", "G0-6C-AA-C12", "G0-SS-AA-C12"], "micro", "flow_cytometry_IL-12_MFI", "supp56")
+
+    tcell = {
+        "supplementary figure 60c": "flow_cytometry_TNF-alpha_CD3_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 60e": "flow_cytometry_IFN-gamma_CD3_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 60g": "flow_cytometry_granzyme_B_CD3_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 61b": "flow_cytometry_TNF-alpha_CD4_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 61d": "flow_cytometry_IFN-gamma_CD4_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 61f": "flow_cytometry_granzyme_B_CD4_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 62b": "flow_cytometry_TNF-alpha_CD8_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 62d": "flow_cytometry_IFN-gamma_CD8_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 62f": "flow_cytometry_granzyme_B_CD8_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 67b": "flow_cytometry_CD3_T_cell_proliferation",
+    }
+    for item, method in tcell.items():
+        if item in SELSET:
+            add_supp(item, ["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 FLuc LNP", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"], "tcell", method, "supp67" if "67" in item else "supp60")
+
+    for item, method in {
+        "supplementary figure 71c": "flow_cytometry_spleen_CD8_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 71d": "flow_cytometry_spleen_CD4_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 71f": "flow_cytometry_spleen_regulatory_T_cells",
+    }.items():
+        if item in SELSET:
+            add_supp(item, ["PBS", "free IL-12 mRNA", "free IDO inhibitor", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12 LNP plus free IDO inhibitor", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"], "invivo", method, "supp71", target="spleen")
+
+    for item, method in {
+        "supplementary figure 78c": "ELISA_IL-6",
+        "supplementary figure 78e": "flow_cytometry_TNF-alpha_CD3_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 78g": "flow_cytometry_IFN-gamma_CD3_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 78i": "flow_cytometry_granzyme_B_CD3_T_cells",
+    }.items():
+        if item in SELSET:
+            add_supp(item, ["PBS", "G0-SS-AA-C12 FLuc pLNP", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12 LNP", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"], "invivo", method, "supp78", target="tumor")
+
+    for item, method in {
+        "supplementary figure 79c": "ELISA_IL-6",
+        "supplementary figure 79d": "ELISA_TNF-alpha",
+        "supplementary figure 79e": "ELISA_IFN-gamma",
+        "supplementary figure 79g": "flow_cytometry_tumor_CD8_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 79i": "flow_cytometry_TNF-alpha_CD3_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 79k": "flow_cytometry_IFN-gamma_CD3_T_cells",
+        "supplementary figure 79m": "flow_cytometry_granzyme_B_CD3_T_cells",
+    }.items():
+        if item in SELSET:
+            add_supp(item, ["PBS", "free IL-12 mRNA", "free IDO inhibitor", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12 LNP plus free IDO inhibitor", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"], "invivo", method, "supp79", target="tumor")
+
+    tox_groups = ["PBS", "free IL-12 mRNA", "free IDO inhibitor", "G0-SS-AA-C12 FLuc pLNP", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12 LNP", "G0-6C-AA-C12 IL-12 LNP plus free IDO inhibitor", "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"]
+    for suffix, method, condkind in [
+        ("b", "ELISA_serum_IL-6", "iv"), ("c", "ELISA_serum_TNF-alpha", "iv"), ("d", "ELISA_serum_IFN-gamma", "iv"),
+        ("e", "ELISA_serum_IL-6", "invivo"), ("f", "ELISA_serum_TNF-alpha", "invivo"), ("g", "ELISA_serum_IFN-gamma", "invivo"),
+    ]:
+        item = "supplementary figure 87" + suffix
+        if item in SELSET:
+            add_supp(item, tox_groups, condkind, method, "supp87", target="serum")
+    for suffix, method in [("h", "ELISA_serum_IL-6"), ("i", "ELISA_serum_TNF-alpha"), ("j", "ELISA_serum_IFN-gamma")]:
+        item = "supplementary figure 87" + suffix
+        if item in SELSET:
+            add_supp(item, ["G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP"], "iv", method, "supp87", target="serum")
+            copy = dict(ROWS[-1])
+            copy["Route_of_administration"] = "intratumoral"
+            ROWS.append(copy)
+    if "supplementary figure 88" in SELSET:
+        add_supp("supplementary figure 88", tox_groups, "iv", "ELISA_AST_ALT", "supp88", target="serum")
+    if "supplementary figure 89" in SELSET:
+        add_supp("supplementary figure 89", tox_groups, "invivo", "ELISA_AST_ALT", "supp89", target="serum")
+
+    if "figure 5h" in SELSET:
+        row = base_row("figure 5h", "scatterplot", "low")
+        cond_invivo(row, "tumor", "RNA-seq")
+        apply_formulation(row, "G0-SS-AA-C12 IL-12 pLNP")
+        row["evidence_text"] = EVID["fig5h"] + " " + EVID["fig5"]
+        row["evidence_image"] = row["source_image"]
+        row["manual_required"] = "true"
+        row["reason"] = "Selected volcano plot does not provide a row-level formulation/value context in Stage 06; retained as manual-review placeholder."
+        add(row)
+
+    represented = {r["Item_ID"].lower() for r in ROWS}
+    for _, selected in SELECTED.iterrows():
+        if selected.item_id.lower() not in represented:
+            row = base_row(clean(selected.item_id), clean(selected.visual_type), "low")
+            add_excel(row, clean(selected.item_id))
+            row["evidence_text"] = clean(selected.reason)
+            row["evidence_image"] = row["source_image"]
+            row["manual_required"] = "true"
+            row["reason"] = "Selected item lacked deterministic condition/formulation extraction rules; placeholder row retained for manual review."
+            add(row)
+
+
+def finalize():
+    for row in ROWS:
+        for col in SMILES_COLS:
+            row[col] = ""
+        if row["Model"] and row["Model"] not in {"in_vitro", "in_vivo", "ex_vivo", "N/A"}:
+            row["Model"] = ""
+            row["manual_required"] = "true"
+            row["reason"] = (row["reason"] + " Invalid Model normalized blank.").strip()
+        if row["metric_type"] and not (row["evidence_excel"] or row["excel_file"] or row["block_csv_path"]):
+            for col in ["metric_type", "original_values", "aggregated_value", "unit", "replicate_type"]:
+                row[col] = ""
+            row["reason"] = (row["reason"] + " Numeric value fields blanked because no Excel/source-data provenance was mapped.").strip()
+
+    stamp = datetime.now().strftime("%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
+    for name in ["unified_extraction.csv", "unified_extraction.json", "unified_extraction_review_flags.csv"]:
+        path = os.path.join(BASE, name)
+        if os.path.exists(path):
+            shutil.copy2(path, path + ".bak_" + stamp)
+
+    pd.DataFrame(ROWS, columns=COLUMNS).to_csv(os.path.join(BASE, "unified_extraction.csv"), index=False, encoding="utf-8-sig")
+
+    flags = []
+    for row in ROWS:
+        if row["manual_required"] == "true":
+            flags.append([PAPER_ID, row["Item_ID"], row["block_id"], "row", "manual_required", "medium", row["reason"] or "Manual review requested."])
+        if not row["evidence_image"]:
+            flags.append([PAPER_ID, row["Item_ID"], row["block_id"], "evidence_image", "missing_figure_evidence", "low", "No source image was available in total_figure_mapping.json."])
+        if not row["Formulation_Name"]:
+            flags.append([PAPER_ID, row["Item_ID"], row["block_id"], "Formulation_Name", "missing_formulation", "medium", "No concise formulation/control label could be extracted."])
+        if not row["Model"]:
+            flags.append([PAPER_ID, row["Item_ID"], row["block_id"], "Model", "missing_condition", "medium", "No concise model context could be extracted."])
+    flags = [list(x) for x in dict.fromkeys(tuple(f) for f in flags)]
+    pd.DataFrame(flags, columns=["Paper_ID", "Item_ID", "block_id", "field", "issue", "severity", "reason"]).to_csv(
+        os.path.join(BASE, "unified_extraction_review_flags.csv"), index=False, encoding="utf-8-sig"
+    )
+
+    summary = {
+        "paper_id": PAPER_ID,
+        "paper_folder": BASE,
+        "stage": "06_unified_lnpdb_extraction",
+        "created_at": datetime.now().isoformat(timespec="seconds"),
+        "record_count": len(ROWS),
+        "selected_item_count": int(len(SELECTED)),
+        "represented_item_count": len({r["Item_ID"].lower() for r in ROWS}),
+        "excel_value_rows": sum(1 for r in ROWS if r["metric_type"]),
+        "smiles_policy": "IL_SMILES, HL_SMILES, CHL_SMILES, PEG_SMILES, and Fifth_component_SMILES intentionally blank for Stage 06.",
+        "sources": [
+            "fig_table_lnpdb_classified.csv",
+            "total_figure_mapping.json",
+            "excel_mapping.json",
+            "excel_mapping_rows.csv",
+            "excel_block_inventory.csv",
+            "QS_2026/QS_2026.md",
+            "41565_2025_2102_MOESM1_ESM/41565_2025_2102_MOESM1_ESM.md",
+        ],
+    }
+    with open(os.path.join(BASE, "unified_extraction.json"), "w", encoding="utf-8") as handle:
+        json.dump({"source_summary": summary, "records": ROWS}, handle, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2)
+    print(json.dumps(summary, ensure_ascii=False, indent=2))
+    print("flags", len(flags))
+
+
+if __name__ == "__main__":
+    generate()
+    finalize()
